 <script>
					var SYWR_DOLLARS_SPENT = '0.10';
					var SYWR_POINTS_OBTAINED = '1';
					var SYWR_DOLLARS_SPENT_THRESHOLD = '0.05';
					var SYWR_DOLLAR_REWARD = '0.01';
					var SYWR_BASE_POINTS = '10';
					var SYWR_REDEMPTION_VALUE = '10';
					var LOYALTY_PINLESS_SERVICE = '';

					function calculatePoints(amountSpent){
						//calculate points from dollars spent
						amountSpent = Math.round(amountSpent*100*100)/100;
						var baseVal = SYWR_DOLLARS_SPENT*100;
						var modVal = amountSpent%baseVal;
						var points = Math.floor(amountSpent/baseVal)*SYWR_POINTS_OBTAINED;
						var roundUpFactor = SYWR_DOLLARS_SPENT_THRESHOLD*100;
						if(modVal >= roundUpFactor){
							points = points + parseInt(SYWR_POINTS_OBTAINED);
						}
						return points;
					}
</script>
